msg:Six reasons to fall in love with this hotel
üõè „ÄêÔ∏èJinan Runhua Crowne Plaza Hotel Check-in Guide„Äë

üìå Hotel Overview Overview

1. Comprehensive evaluation (highlights, shortcomings, regrets): 

üè® About the guest room In Room

1. Guest room layout and hardware evaluation (is the room large): The hotel helped me upgrade to an open-plan suite in the corner, with a good view and a large area. It is equipped with a bathtub, a Leffen hair dryer, a steam hand-held iron and an air purifier. The most eye-catching thing is the light blue Italian SMEG coffee machine and kettle. The ceiling of beauty is not covered, which adds a lot of color to the fashionable tone of the whole house. This is the second reason why I like this hotel: the guest room layout is reasonable, the details are rich, and the sincerity is full.

‚òïÔ∏è Dining

1. Hotel breakfast variety and service (good or not): The excellence of catering is almost their biggest feature, and it is remarkable everywhere. It is no exaggeration to say that among the 420 Crowne Plaza brand hotels in the world, their breakfast and executive lounge products are top-notch. If they keep up, it is not impossible to be upgraded to Indigo one day. The full-day design combines the elegant pattern of spring breeze and Yishui with the trendy elements of childish fun. It is both solemn and humorous, suitable for all ages, and has an excellent balance between grace and rhythm. The layout of the fruit and cold plate area is similar to that of Indigo in Tianmu Mountain, which is green and vibrant. There are many options for freshly squeezed juice. The steaming area has local snacks and containers (wooden boxes). The super-large pot of steaming Cordyceps soup matrix has a strong visual impact. The noodles, toppings and soups of the noodle stall are definitely in the first camp among the 123 CPs in China, such as the rare purple potato noodles, etc. There is a special dining area for diamond members. Although there is no special compar**ent like the Crowne Plaza in Beihai, it is still the best position in the restaurant, and a sense of respect arises suddenly. The products of the Executive Lounge Happy Hour are also not inferior, especially the shapes of several desserts, which are comparable to those of the pastry chefs of Guihe IC. They are delicious and pleasing to the eyes, allowing the body and mind that are tired for a day to get 360-degree, all-round relaxation of the five senses. This is the third reason why I like this store: with completely superior catering quality, the journey of gluttony is not only completed in Kimpton. Now, the business-oriented Crowne Plaza (once upon a time, this brand was so standard, standard, and old-fashioned, and the new generation of CP has undoubtedly given this brand a new life and dignity) can also take the lead, which is gratifying.

üèä Hardware Facilities

1. Hotel environment: The fourth reason for liking this hotel is that it is too new. All aspects (high-altitude lobby, first-floor water system, entrance hall, public area bar, etc.) have adopted the latest design and decoration standards of Crowne Plaza, resonating with the most cutting-edge thoughts of this era, which is really a beautiful thing. The hotel was soft-opened on December 31 last year and officially opened on March 31 this year. With several months of operational experience, the hotel is about to enter a colorful mature period. To be honest, the background of "hospitable Shandong" and its profound cultural heritage are particularly suitable for Huayu to be listed. It's a pity that at present, only Qingdao, which has a relatively shallow history, has Huayu layout in the land of Qilu. The provincial capital of Quancheng really needs Huayu to respond and care. This is the hometown of the great poets Li Qingzhao and Xin Qiji that we miss so much. Even Mr. Lao She, a literary giant from Beijing, regards Jinan as his second hometown. Therefore, the city's abundant tourism resources and cultural resources are absolutely worthy of having a Huayu. Of course, this is just my personal opinion and simple imagination; in fact, the hotel has thought about the national style, such as the setting of tea ceremony in the lobby public area, which is a combination of Chinese and Western styles, which is very good.

üåü Unforgettable Moments
1. Outstanding performance and awards of star employees (whether the service is strong): Xiaona, the duty manager, arranged my entire travel cycle properly and naturally (the welcome snacks and desserts in the room are very local, and she is thoughtful; she will take the initiative to make freshly ground coffee for me when welcoming and seeing off guests, and she knows the hard work of business trips like us; not every hotel butler will lead guests to the room and explain all the details of the room when the guests just check in, she did it; not every hotel butler will send guests to the car and wave goodbye when the guests check out, she did it), thank you very much. The fifth reason for liking this hotel is naturally because of these excellent benchmark employees of Runhua Group. From 2006 to the present, from Jinan Convention and Exhibition Center to Shandong International Convention and Exhibition Center, in a blink of an eye, I have hosted the Qilu Auto Show for the 19th time. In addition to its achievements in real estate and hotel industries, Runhua Group is also one of the leaders in the field of automobile dealers in Shandong Province. Most well-known automobile brands have maintained close cooperation with Runhua. The opening of this hotel is obviously convenient for business travelers and guests attending exhibitions in the automotive industry, especially for holding various automotive conferences, releases, and activities. For example, during my stay, the regional joint work meeting of Lexus North China and Northeast China was in full swing in the hotel. This kind of closed-loop construction of the whole ecosystem is definitely an expert in Runhua.

üìç Brief summary Conclusion

1. Wonderful moments of the journey: The last point that I love deeply in this hotel is the gym. The equipment is advanced and complete, the swimming pool water is clean, the yoga room is spacious and transparent, and the details of the layout and binding are ingenious (such as elephant-shaped towels, fruit baskets, etc.). After sweating profusely, you will fall in love with this hotel more and more (the successful creation of the repeat stay rate comes from this). In summary, every bit of Runhua CP touches the softest part of your soul. On the journey, it is necessary to be good to yourself. Fortunately, Runhua Crowne Plaza has helped us do it. Thank you.
